We introduce memory decoupling to separate persistent observations from transient execution context, and train the policy agent to selectively invoke the copilot as Retriever or Calculator based on task demands. ### [111] [Beyond State Consistency: Behavior Consistency in Text-Based World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13824)
*Youling Huang,Guanqiao Chen,Junchi Yao,Lu Wang,Fangkai Yang,Chao Du,ChenZhuo Zhao,Pu Zhao,Qingwei Lin,Saravan Rajmohan,Dongmei Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种新的行为对齐训练范式，通过优化行为一致性奖励（BehR）来改进世界模型与真实环境之间的功能一致性，在文本环境中提升了长期对齐性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本环境中世界模型的评估和训练通常使用单步指标（如精确匹配），但这些指标已被证明不足以捕捉实际智能体行为。需要一种能够更好评估世界模型与真实环境功能一致性的方法。

Method: 提出行为对齐训练范式，优化名为行为一致性奖励（BehR）的可处理步级指标。BehR测量在冻结参考智能体下，记录的下一个动作在真实状态与世界模型预测状态之间的似然变化程度。

Result: 在WebShop和TextWorld上的实验表明，基于BehR的训练在多个设置中改善了长期对齐，在WebShop中效果最明显，在接近天花板区域变化较小。在四个设置中的三个中保持或改善了单步预测质量。使用BehR训练的世界模型在离线代理评估中实现了更低的误报率，并在推理时前瞻规划中显示出适度但令人鼓舞的改进。

Conclusion: 行为对齐训练范式通过优化行为一致性奖励，有效提升了世界模型与真实环境之间的功能一致性，为文本环境中的世界模型训练提供了更有效的评估和优化方法。

Abstract: World models have been emerging as critical components for assessing the consequences of actions generated by interactive agents in online planning and offline evaluation. In text-based environments, world models are typically evaluated and trained with single-step metrics such as Exact Match, aiming to improve the similarity between predicted and real-world states, but such metrics have been shown to be insufficient for capturing actual agent behavior. To address this issue, we introduce a new behavior-aligned training paradigm aimed at improving the functional consistency between the world model and the real environment. This paradigm focuses on optimizing a tractable step-level metric named Behavior Consistency Reward (BehR), which measures how much the likelihood of a logged next action changes between the real state and the world-model-predicted state under a frozen Reference Agent. Experiments on WebShop and TextWorld show that BehR-based training improves long-term alignment in several settings, with the clearest gains in WebShop and less movement in near-ceiling regimes, while preserving or improving single-step prediction quality in three of four settings. World models trained with BehR also achieve lower false positives in offline surrogate evaluation and show modest but encouraging gains in inference-time lookahead planning.

</details>


### [112] [Simulation-Based Optimisation of Batting Order and Bowling Plans in T20 Cricket](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13861)
*Tinniam V Ganesh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文开发了一个统一的MDP框架，用于优化T20板球比赛中的击球顺序选择和投球计划分配，直接基于获胜/防守概率而非预期得分。使用三阶段球员档案引擎和James-Stein收缩方法，通过向量化蒙特卡洛模拟评估概率，并应用于2026年IPL比赛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统板球决策优化通常基于预期得分，但比赛结果更直接地取决于获胜或防守概率。现有方法往往忽略比赛不同阶段（强力击球、中场、死亡阶段）球员表现的差异，导致决策次优化。需要开发一个统一框架，直接优化获胜/防守概率，并考虑阶段特异性球员表现。

Method: 1. 建立统一的马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）框架，直接优化获胜和防守概率；2. 开发三阶段球员档案引擎（强力击球、中场、死亡阶段），使用James-Stein收缩方法从1,161个IPL逐球记录（2008-2025）估计球员表现；3. 通过向量化蒙特卡洛模拟（N=50,000局轨迹）评估获胜/防守概率；4. 击球顺序通过穷举枚举搜索；5. 投球计划通过模拟退火算法计算，考虑剩余配额约束且同一投球手不能连续投球。

Result: 应用于2026年IPL两场比赛：1. 最优击球顺序将孟买印度人队的获胜概率提高了4.1个百分点（从52.4%到56.5%）；2. 最优古吉拉特泰坦队投球计划将防守概率提高了5.2个百分点（从39.1%到44.3%）。次优化决策与阶段无关的部署一致，这些决策在聚合指标下看似合理，但在应用阶段特异性档案时显示出成本高昂。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于阶段特异性球员档案直接优化获胜/防守概率的MDP框架的有效性。相比传统基于预期得分的方法，该框架能显著提高比赛决策质量。研究结果强调了考虑比赛不同阶段球员表现差异的重要性，为板球战术决策提供了更精确的优化工具。

Abstract: This paper develops a unified Markov Decision Process (MDP) framework for optimising two recurring in-match decisions in T20 cricket namely batting order selection and bowling plan assignment, directly in terms of win and defend probability rather than expected runs. A three-phase player profile engine (Powerplay, Middle, Death) with James-Stein shrinkage is estimated from 1,161 IPL ball-by-ball records (2008-2025). Win/defend probabilities are evaluated by vectorised Monte Carlo simulation over N = 50,000 innings trajectories. Batting orders are searched by exhaustive enumeration. Bowling plans are computed by simulated annealing over the remaining quota with the constraint that the same bowler cannot bowl consecutive overs. Applied to two 2026 IPL matches, the optimal batting order improves Mumbai Indians' win probability by 4.1 percentage points (52.4% to 56.5%), and the optimal Gujarat Titans bowling plan improves defend probability by 5.2 percentage points (39.1% to 44.3%). In both cases the observed sub-optimality is consistent with phase-agnostic deployment in decisions that appear reasonable by aggregate metrics but are exposed as costly when phase-specific profiles are applied.

*Eymen Ipek*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决深度神经网络在安全关键、资源受限环境中的两个结构缺陷：1）学习函数的不透明性阻碍形式化验证；2）异构激活函数依赖导致边缘硬件延迟和面积开销增加。

Method: 将EML算子嵌入传统DNN架构，形成混合模型：主干学习分布式表示，头部是深度受限、权重稀疏的EML树，其截断权重可折叠为闭式符号子表达式。

Result: 推导前向方程，证明计算成本边界，分析相对于MLP和PINN的推理和训练加速，量化FPGA/模拟部署的权衡。在定制EML单元上可实现数量级的延迟优势，同时提升可解释性和形式化验证可行性。

Conclusion: DNN-EML组合填补了文献空白，虽然不太可能加速训练或在通用CPU/GPU上加速推理，但在定制硬件上可实现显著延迟优势，同时增强可解释性和形式化验证能力。

Abstract: Deep neural networks (DNNs) deliver state-of-the-art accuracy on regression and classification tasks, yet two structural deficits persistently obstruct their deployment in safety-critical, resource-constrained settings: (i) opacity of the learned function, which precludes formal verification, and (ii) reliance on heterogeneous, library-bound activation functions that inflate latency and silicon area on edge hardware. The recently introduced Exp-Minus-Log (EML) Sheffer operator, eml(x, y) = exp(x) - ln(y), was shown by Odrzywolek (2026) to be sufficient - together with the constant 1 - to express every standard elementary function as a binary tree of identical nodes. We propose to embed EML primitives inside conventional DNN architectures, yielding a hybrid DNN-EML model in which the trunk learns distributed representations and the head is a depth-bounded, weight-sparse EML tree whose snapped weights collapse to closed-form symbolic sub-expressions. We derive the forward equations, prove computational-cost bounds, analyse inference and training acceleration relative to multilayer perceptrons (MLPs) and physics-informed neural networks (PINNs), and quantify the trade-offs for FPGA/analog deployment. We argue that the DNN-EML pairing closes a literature gap: prior neuro-symbolic and equation-learner approaches (EQL, KAN, AI-Feynman) work with heterogeneous primitive sets and do not exploit a single hardware-realisable Sheffer element. A balanced assessment shows that EML is unlikely to accelerate training, and on commodity CPU/GPU it is also unlikely to accelerate inference; however, on a custom EML cell (FPGA logic block or analog circuit) the asymptotic latency advantage can reach an order of magnitude with simultaneous gain in interpretability and formal-verification tractability.

</details>

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has catalyzed significant advances in the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, effectively managing the exploration and exploitation trade-off remains a critical challenge. In this paper, we fully analyze the exploration and exploitation dilemma of extremely hard and easy samples during the training and propose a new fine-grained trade-off mechanism. Concretely, we introduce a perplexity space disentangling strategy that divides the sample space into distinct exploration (high perplexity) and exploitation (low perplexity) subspaces, thereby mining fine-grained samples requiring exploration-exploitation trade-off. Subsequently, we propose a bidirectional reward allocation mechanism with a minimum impact on verification rewards to implement perplexity-guided exploration and exploitation, enabling more stable policy optimization.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study value adaptation in offline-to-online reinforcement learning under general function approximation. Starting from an imperfect offline pretrained $Q$-function, the learner aims to adapt it to the target environment using only a limited amount of online interaction. We first characterize the difficulty of this setting by establishing a minimax lower bound, showing that even when the pretrained $Q$-function is close to optimal $Q^\star$, online adaptation can be no more efficient than pure online RL on certain hard instances. Finally, we complement our theory with neural-network experiments that demonstrate the practical effectiveness of the proposed method.

Motivation: 在计算机中预测细胞状态扰动效应可以大规模识别细胞行为驱动因素并加速药物发现，但单细胞基因表达的固有异质性和复杂的潜在基因依赖性给建模带来了挑战。

Method: PRiMeFlow采用端到端的流匹配方法，直接在基因表达空间中建模遗传和小分子扰动效应。该方法使用分布拟合方法，通过U-Net架构参数化速度场。

Result: 在PerturBench中进行广泛基准测试表明，PRiMeFlow能够准确近似单细胞基因表达的经验分布。消融研究验证了在基因表达空间中操作和使用U-Net架构参数化速度场等重要设计选择。该架构为基础构建的模型在首届ARC虚拟细胞挑战赛中获得了通用奖。

Conclusion: PRiMeFlow通过流匹配方法有效解决了单细胞基因表达建模的挑战，为预测遗传和小分子扰动效应提供了准确的计算框架，在细胞行为研究和药物发现中具有应用潜力。

Abstract: Predicting the effects of perturbations in-silico on cell state can identify drivers of cell behavior at scale and accelerate drug discovery. However, modeling challenges remain due to the inherent heterogeneity of single cell gene expression and the complex, latent gene dependencies. Here, we present PRiMeFlow, an end-to-end flow matching based approach to directly model the effects of genetic and small molecule perturbations in the gene expression space. The distribution-fitting approach taken by PRiMeFlow enables it to accurately approximate the empirical distribution of single-cell gene expression, which we demonstrate through extensive benchmarking inside PerturBench. Through ablation studies, we also validate important model design choices such as operating in gene expression space and parameterizing the velocity field with a U-Net architecture. The PRiMeFlow architecture was used as the basis for the model that won the Generalist Prize in the first ARC Virtual Cell Challenge.

</details>


### [121] [Unsupervised domain transfer: Overcoming signal degradation in sleep monitoring by increasing scoring realism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13988)
*Mohammad Ahangarkiasari,Andreas Tind Damgaard,Casper Haurum,Kaare B. Mikkelsen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种基于判别器引导微调的无监督方法，用于处理移动睡眠监测中的信号退化问题，通过将目标域特征与预训练特征空间对齐来适应不同类型的信号失真。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 移动睡眠监测中常遇到各种信号退化问题，但为每种退化类型设计专门的监督模型不切实际。本研究旨在探索利用睡眠分期图（hypnogram）的"真实性"来指导无监督方法，以处理任意类型的信号退化。

Method: 结合预训练的u-sleep模型和判别器网络，将目标域特征与预训练期间学习的特征空间对齐。通过向源域添加真实的信号退化来测试方法对不同类型退化的适应能力，并与针对每种转移设计的监督模型进行比较。

Result: 无监督方法能提高Cohen's kappa值（提升范围0.03-0.29），且在所有转移中均未降低性能。但该方法从未达到理论最优性能，在真实睡眠研究数据上的域不匹配测试中，改善效果不显著。

Conclusion: 判别器引导微调是处理"野外"睡眠监测信号退化的有前景方法，但需要进一步开发才能用于实际生产环境。该方法对睡眠数据的普遍性提供了有趣见解。

Abstract: Objective: Investigate whether hypnogram 'realism' can be used to guide an unsupervised method for handling arbitrary types of signal degradation in mobile sleep monitoring.
  Approach: Combining a pretrained, state-of-the-art 'u-sleep' model with a 'discriminator' network, we align features from a target domain with a feature space learned during pretraining. To test the approach, we distort the source domain with realistic signal degradations, to see how well the method can adapt to different types of degradation. We compare the performance of the resulting model with best-case models designed in a supervised manner for each type of transfer.
  Main Results: Depending on the type of distortion, we find that the unsupervised approach can increase Cohen's kappa with as little as 0.03 and up to 0.29, and that for all transfers, the method does not decrease performance. However, the approach never quite reaches the estimated theoretical optimal performance, and when tested on a real-life domain mismatch between two sleep studies, the benefit was insignificant.
  Significance: 'Discriminator-guided fine tuning' is an interesting approach to handling signal degradation for 'in the wild' sleep monitoring, with some promise. In particular, what it says about sleep data in general is interesting. However, more development will be necessary before using it 'in production'.

*Mohammad Nooraiepour,Zezhang Song,Wei Li,Sarah Perez*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用物理信息迁移学习框架：1) 通过弹性权重巩固将氢吸附PINN迁移到甲烷吸附预测；2) 煤质特征工程；3) 三阶段课程学习平衡迁移保持与热力学微调；4) 评估五种贝叶斯不确定性量化方法（蒙特卡洛Dropout、深度集成等）；5) 使用SHAP和ALE进行特征可解释性分析。

Result: 在114个独立煤实验的993个平衡测量数据上，框架达到R²=0.932，比仅基于压力的经典等温线提升227%；氢预训练比随机初始化降低18.9% RMSE并加速19.4%收敛；蒙特卡洛Dropout在物理约束架构中表现最佳，而深度集成因共享物理约束导致性能下降；特征分析显示学习表示保持物理可解释性。

Conclusion: 蒙特卡洛Dropout是该物理约束迁移学习框架中最佳的不确定性量化方法，跨气体迁移学习是地质材料建模的数据高效策略，学习表示与煤吸附机制保持一致，为异质煤阶甲烷吸附预测提供了热力学一致、可迁移且具有校准不确定性的综合解决方案。

Abstract: Accurate methane sorption prediction across heterogeneous coal ranks requires models that combine thermodynamic consistency, efficient knowledge transfer across data-scarce geological systems, and calibrated uncertainty estimates, capabilities that are rarely addressed together in existing frameworks. Trained on 993 equilibrium measurements from 114 independent coal experiments spanning lignite to anthracite, the framework achieves R2 = 0.932 on held-out coal samples, a 227% improvement over pressure-only classical isotherms, while hydrogen pre-training delivers 18.9% lower RMSE and 19.4% faster convergence than random initialization. Five Bayesian uncertainty quantification approaches reveal a systematic divergence in performance across physics-constrained architectures. Monte Carlo Dropout achieves well-calibrated uncertainty at minimal overhead, while deep ensembles, regardless of architectural diversity or initialization strategy, exhibit performance degradation because shared physics constraints narrow the admissible solution manifold. SHAP and ALE analyses confirm that learned representations remain physically interpretable and aligned with established coal sorption mechanisms: moisture-volatile interactions are most influential, pressure-temperature coupling captures thermodynamic co-dependence, and features exhibit non-monotonic effects. These results identify Monte Carlo Dropout as the best-performing UQ method in this physics-constrained transfer learning framework, and demonstrate cross-gas transfer learning as a data-efficient strategy for geological material modeling.

### [123] [Parameter Importance is Not Static: Evolving Parameter Isolation for Supervised Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14010)
*Zekai Lin,Chao Xue,Di Liang,Xingsheng Han,Peiyang Liu,Xianjie Wu,Lei Jiang,Yu Lu,Haibo Shi,Shuang Liang,Minlong Peng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EPI提出动态参数隔离框架，通过在线评估参数重要性并周期性更新隔离掩码，解决传统静态隔离方法无法适应训练过程中参数重要性漂移的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 监督微调存在任务干扰和灾难性遗忘问题，现有静态参数隔离方法假设参数重要性固定不变，但实际训练中参数重要性会随时间漂移，需要动态适应机制。

Method: 提出演化参数隔离(EPI)框架，基于梯度信号在线评估参数重要性，周期性更新隔离掩码，保护新出现的任务关键参数，同时释放过时参数以恢复模型可塑性。

Result: 在多任务基准测试中，EPI相比静态隔离和标准微调，能持续减少干扰和遗忘，同时提升整体泛化能力。

Conclusion: 隔离机制需要与学习动态演化同步，动态参数隔离能有效应对训练过程中参数重要性的变化，提升多任务学习效果。

Abstract: Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) of large language models often suffers from task interference and catastrophic forgetting. Recent approaches alleviate this issue by isolating task-critical parameters during training. However, these methods represent a static solution to a dynamic problem, assuming that parameter importance remains fixed once identified. In this work, we empirically demonstrate that parameter importance exhibits temporal drift over the course of training. To address this, we propose Evolving Parameter Isolation (EPI), a fine-tuning framework that adapts isolation decisions based on online estimates of parameter importance. Instead of freezing a fixed subset of parameters, EPI periodically updates isolation masks using gradient-based signals, enabling the model to protect emerging task-critical parameters while releasing outdated ones to recover plasticity. Experiments on diverse multi-task benchmarks demonstrate that EPI consistently reduces interference and forgetting compared to static isolation and standard fine-tuning, while improving overall generalization. Our analysis highlights the necessity of synchronizing isolation mechanisms with the evolving dynamics of learning diverse abilities.

</details>


### [124] [A Complete Symmetry Classification of Shallow ReLU Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14037)
*Pranavkrishnan Ramakrishnan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了ReLU激活函数下浅层神经网络的参数空间对称性，提供了完整的分类方法


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络参数空间与函数空间并不等同，存在不同参数实现相同函数的情况（参数对称性）。虽然早期研究已关注此问题，但现有分类方法需要激活函数的解析性，无法处理重要的ReLU激活函数（非可微）。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 利用ReLU激活函数的非可微性，对浅层神经网络（shallow case）的参数对称性进行完整分类。通过分析神经流形（neuromanifold）的几何结构，识别产生相同函数的不同参数。

Result: 提供了ReLU激活函数下浅层神经网络参数对称性的完整分类。这一结果扩展了先前仅限于解析激活函数的研究，首次系统处理了非可微的ReLU情况。

Conclusion: ReLU激活函数的非可微性反而成为分析参数对称性的有利工具，使得对浅层神经网络参数空间对称性的完整分类成为可能。这一研究为理解神经流形的几何结构及其对优化动力学的影响提供了新视角。

Abstract: Parameter space is not function space for neural network architectures. This fact, investigated as early as the 1990s under terms such as ``reverse engineering," or ``parameter identifiability", has led to the natural question of parameter space symmetries\textemdash the study of distinct parameters in neural architectures which realize the same function. Indeed, the quotient space obtained by identifying parameters giving rise to the same function, called the \textit{neuromanifold}, has been shown in some cases to have rich geometric properties, impacting optimization dynamics. Thus far, techniques towards complete classifications have required the analyticity of the activation function, notably excising the important case of ReLU. Here, in contrast, we exploit the non-differentiability of the ReLU activation to provide a complete classification of the symmetries in the shallow case.

</details>


### [125] [$π$-Play: Multi-Agent Self-Play via Privileged Self-Distillation without External Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14054)
*Yaocheng Zhang,Yuanheng Zhu,Wenyue Chong,Songjun Tu,Qichao Zhang,Jiajun Chai,Xiaohan Wang,Wei Lin,Guojun Yin,Dongbin Zhao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度搜索代理训练面临稀疏奖励、弱信用分配和有限标注数据等挑战。传统自博弈仅通过稀疏结果奖励优化学生模型，学习效率低下。作者发现自博弈过程中自然产生的问题构造路径(QCP)可作为特权信息，为教师模型提供高质量监督信号。

Method: 提出特权信息自博弈(π-Play)框架：1)考官生成任务及其QCP；2)教师模型利用QCP作为特权上下文，通过自蒸馏密集监督学生模型；3)将传统稀疏奖励自博弈转变为密集反馈自进化循环。

Result: 实验表明，无数据的π-Play框架超越了完全监督的搜索代理，并将进化效率比传统自博弈提升了2-3倍。

Conclusion: 自博弈过程中自然产生的QCP可作为高质量特权信息，π-Play框架通过利用这一发现实现了高效的密集反馈自进化，显著提升了深度搜索代理的训练效率。

Abstract: Deep search agents have emerged as a promising paradigm for addressing complex information-seeking tasks, but their training remains challenging due to sparse rewards, weak credit assignment, and limited labeled data. Self-play offers a scalable route to reduce data dependence, but conventional self-play optimizes students only through sparse outcome rewards, leading to low learning efficiency. In this work, we observe that self-play naturally produces a question construction path (QCP) during task generation, an intermediate artifact that captures the reverse solution process. This reveals a new source of privileged information for self-distillation: self-play can itself provide high-quality privileged context for the teacher model in a low-cost and scalable manner, without relying on human feedback or curated privileged information. Leveraging this insight, we propose Privileged Information Self-Play ($π$-Play), a multi-agent self-evolution framework. In $π$-Play, an examiner generates tasks together with their QCPs, and a teacher model leverages QCP as privileged context to densely supervise a student via self-distillation. This design transforms conventional sparse-reward self-play into a dense-feedback self-evolution loop. Extensive experiments show that data-free $π$-Play surpasses fully supervised search agents and improves evolutionary efficiency by 2-3$\times$ over conventional self-play.

Abstract: Resolving and rewriting references is fundamental in programming languages. We introduce new sequence-to-sequence architectures for both problems. Our measurements show that our architectures outperform the baselines in both robustness and scalability: our models can handle examples that are ten times longer compared to the best baseline. We measure the impact of our architecture in the real-world task of decompiling switch statements, which has an indexing subtask. ### [127] [Complex Interpolation of Matrices with an application to Multi-Manifold Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.14118)
*Adi Arbel,Stefan Steinerberger,Ronen Talmon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究对称正定矩阵插值A^{1-x}B^x的谱性质，发现算子范数精确对数线性等价于原矩阵存在共享特征向量，近似对数线性则迫使主奇异向量与两矩阵主导特征向量对齐，为多流形学习提供理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究对称正定矩阵A和B的插值A^{1-x}B^x的谱性质，旨在探究矩阵间"共同结构"的存在性，即特征向量指向相似方向的情况，为多视图数据中共同和独特潜在结构的识别提供数学基础。

Method: 采用矩阵插值方法，研究A^{1-x}B^x在x∈[0,1]区间上的谱性质，分析算子范数‖A^{1-x}B^x‖的对数线性特性，建立精确对数线性与共享特征向量存在的等价关系，推导近似对数线性时的稳定性界限。

Result: 精确对数线性等价于原矩阵存在共享特征向量；近似对数线性迫使主奇异向量与两矩阵主导特征向量对齐；这些结果为多流形学习框架提供理论依据，能够识别多视图数据中的共同和独特潜在结构。

Conclusion: 矩阵插值方法为分析对称正定矩阵间的结构相似性提供了有效工具，算子范数的对数线性特性直接反映了矩阵间的共同特征结构，这一理论框架为多视图数据分析和多流形学习提供了坚实的数学基础。

Abstract: Given two symmetric positive-definite matrices $A, B \in \mathbb{R}^{n \times n}$, we study the spectral properties of the interpolation $A^{1-x} B^x$ for $0 \leq x \leq 1$. The presence of `common structures' in $A$ and $B$, eigenvectors pointing in a similar direction, can be investigated using this interpolation perspective. Generically, exact log-linearity of the operator norm $\|A^{1-x} B^x\|$ is equivalent to the existence of a shared eigenvector in the original matrices; stability bounds show that approximate log-linearity forces principal singular vectors to align with leading eigenvectors of both matrices. These results give rise to and provide theoretical justification for a multi-manifold learning framework that identifies common and distinct latent structures in multiview data.

</details>

### [128] [HUANet: Hard-Constrained Unrolled ADMM for Constrained Convex Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13179)
*Trinh Tran,Binh Nguyen,Truong X. Nghiem*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: HUANet：一种将ADMM迭代展开为可训练神经网络的约束深度网络架构，用于求解约束凸优化问题


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端学习方法作为从参数到解决方案的黑盒映射，通常缺乏明确的最优性原理且无法强制执行约束

Method: 将ADMM迭代展开为可训练神经网络，在每次迭代中嵌入硬约束神经网络以加速算法，通过可微分校正阶段在输出端强制等式约束，并在训练中将一阶最优性条件作为软约束以促进收敛

Result: 广泛的数值实验验证了所提架构对约束优化问题的有效性

Conclusion: HUANet通过将ADMM展开为可训练神经网络，结合硬约束和软约束机制，为约束凸优化问题提供了一种具有明确最优性原理且能有效执行约束的深度学习解决方案

Abstract: This paper presents HUANet, a constrained deep neural network architecture that unrolls the iterations of the Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers (ADMM) into a trainable neural network for solving constrained convex optimization problems. Existing end-to-end learning methods operate as black-box mappings from parameters to solutions, often lacking explicit optimality principles and failing to enforce constraints. To address this limitation, we unroll ADMM and embed a hard-constrained neural network at each iteration to accelerate the algorithm, where equality constraints are enforced via a differentiable correction stage at the network output. Furthermore, we incorporate first-order optimality conditions as soft constraints during training to promote the convergence of the proposed unrolled algorithm. Extensive numerical experiments are conducted to validate the effectiveness of the proposed architecture for constrained optimization problems.

</details>


### [129] [A Momentum-based Stochastic Algorithm for Linearly Constrained Nonconvex Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13272)
*Chenyang Qiu,Mihitha Maithripala,Zongli Lin*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出一种基于动量的增广拉格朗日方法，用于求解带线性约束的非凸随机优化问题，每迭代仅需一次随机梯度评估，达到ε-平稳解的期望复杂度为O(ε⁻⁴)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决带线性约束的非凸随机优化问题，其中目标函数光滑但只能获得有界方差的随机梯度。现有方法通常需要多次梯度评估或收敛保证不足，需要开发更高效的算法。

Method: 提出动量增强的增广拉格朗日方法，采用Polyak型梯度估计器，每迭代仅需一次随机梯度评估。算法结合动量技术加速收敛，处理线性约束通过增广拉格朗日框架。

Result: 在标准随机oracle模型和期望目标光滑性条件下，建立了原始约束问题一阶KKT残差的收敛保证。算法在期望意义下以O(ε⁻⁴)随机梯度评估计算ε-平稳解。数值实验显示相比代表性递归动量基线具有竞争力的迭代复杂度和改进的墙钟效率。

Conclusion: 提出的动量增广拉格朗日方法为带线性约束的非凸随机优化提供了高效解决方案，单次梯度评估设计降低了计算成本，理论保证和实验验证了其优越性能。

Abstract: This paper studies a stochastic algorithm for linearly constrained nonconvex optimization, where the objective function is smooth but only unbiased stochastic gradients with bounded variance are available. We propose a momentum-based augmented Lagrangian method that employs a Polyak-type gradient estimator and requires only one stochastic gradient evaluation per iteration. Under the standard stochastic oracle model and the smoothness condition of the expected objective, we establish a convergence guarantee in terms of the first-order KKT residual of the original constrained problem. In particular, the proposed method computes an $ε$-stationary solution in expectation within $O(ε^{-4})$ stochastic gradient evaluations. Numerical experiments further show that the proposed method achieves competitive iteration complexity and improved wall-clock efficiency compared with representative recursive-momentum baselines.

### [130] [A simple approach to the Løkka-Zervos dichotomy for absolutely continuous dividend strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13302)

Abstract: We revisit the optimization problem solved in Løkka & Zervos (2008), i.e., the maximization of dividends, in a Brownian risk model, with the possibility (not the obligation) of making capital injections. Following the approach introduced in Alvarez & Shepp (1998), Renaud & Simard (2021), Renaud et al. (2023), we consider instead absolutely continuous (AC) dividend strategies with an affine bound on the payment rates, while singular capital injections are still allowed. In addition, we incorporate a parameter for the cost of ruin or, said differently, a penalty at ruin in the performance function. We show that the solution is a so-called Løkka-Zervos dichotomy: the surplus is never ruined by making bail-out payments, or no capital is injected and bankruptcy can occur; in either case, dividends are paid at full rate when the surplus is above a threshold. Our framework allows us to provide explicit conditions to express the dichotomy, either using the cost of capital injections or the cost of ruin as a criterion, which also exposes the underlying structure of the solution. In particular, for some values of the parameters, we show that it is optimal to liquidate. Moreover, we perform a numerical analysis highlighting the range of values generated under this AC affine-bound structure.

Exploiting the monotone depletion of susceptible populations, we construct a robust terminal set and safe backup policy. This structure ensures recursive feasibility and finite-horizon closed-loop exponential decay, and it certifies the existence of a globally stabilizing feasible continuation under bounded worst-case transmission rates. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有非凸优化理论主要围绕梯度动态，全局收敛性研究不足。主导范式关注平稳性（梯度范数消失），但这常是优化成功的弱代理指标。实践中梯度范数可能停滞或增加，平稳点可能远离全局解。

Method: 重新审视Ball Proximal Point Method (BPM)，提出新的结构条件Broximal Alignment。该条件无需凸性、光滑性或Lipschitz假设，允许存在多个且不连通的全局最小值以及非最优局部最小值。

Result: 证明在Broximal Alignment条件下，BPM能收敛到全局最小化器。该条件推广了标准非凸框架，如拟凸性、星凸性、类星凸性和aiming条件。

Abstract: Most non-convex optimization theory is built around gradient dynamics, leaving global convergence largely unexplored. The dominant paradigm focuses on stationarity, certifying only that the gradient norm vanishes, which is often a weak proxy for actual optimization success. In practice, gradient norms can stagnate or even increase during training, and stationary points may be far from global solutions. In this work, we propose a new framework for global non-convex optimization that avoids gradient-based reasoning altogether. We revisit the Ball Proximal Point Method (BPM), a trust-region-style algorithm introduced by Gruntkowska et al. (2025), and propose a novel structural condition - Broximal Alignment - under which BPM provably converges to a global minimizer. Our condition requires no convexity, smoothness, or Lipschitz assumptions, and it permits multiple and disconnected global minima as well as non-optimal local minima. ### [137] [Semidefinite relaxations for nonlinear elasticity with energies convex in the Cauchy-Green strain tensor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13566)
*Didier Henrion,Milan Korda,Martin Kružík,Karolına Sehnalová*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在非线性弹性中，对于满足特定条件的非凸能量函数，原始变分问题与其基于占据测度的线性矩表述之间不存在松弛间隙，从而保证了Lasserre矩-SOS层次结构的收敛性，提供了一种无网格、计算高效的数值方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非线性弹性中，最小化存储能量密度的材料变形问题是一个具有挑战性的变分问题，可能不存在极小值解——能量最优的材料会形成无限精细的微观结构（褶皱）而非平滑变形。传统有限元方法会产生不期望的网格依赖伪影，需要开发更有效的数值方法。

Method: 使用Le Dret-Raoult半定投影公式计算能量函数的拟凸包络，证明原始非凸变分问题与其基于占据测度的线性矩表述之间不存在松弛间隙。利用Lasserre矩-平方和（SOS）层次结构，提供无网格的数值计算方法。在边界条件线性且函数在应变张量中SOS凸的附加条件下，证明Lasserre层次结构的第一级松弛是精确的。

Result: 证明了对于满足框架无关性且在Cauchy-Green应变张量中凸的非凸能量函数，原始变分问题与线性矩表述之间不存在松弛间隙。这保证了Lasserre矩-SOS层次结构的收敛性，提供了一种计算高效、无网格的数值方法，避免了有限元方法的网格依赖伪影。在附加条件下，计算拟凸包络简化为求解一个小型凸半定优化问题。

Conclusion: 该研究为非线性弹性中的变分问题提供了一种新的理论框架和计算方法。通过证明松弛间隙为零，确保了Lasserre矩-SOS层次结构的收敛性，从而能够有效地计算能量函数的拟凸包络。这种方法避免了传统有限元方法的网格依赖问题，为处理材料微观结构形成问题提供了更可靠的数值工具。

Abstract: In nonlinear elasticity, finding the deformation of a material which minimizes a given stored energy density is a challenging calculus of variations problem which may fail to have minimizers: the energy optimal material forms infinitely fine microstructures (wrinkles) rather than deforming smoothly. In the case where the energy function is non-convex but frame indifferent and convex with respect to the Cauchy-Green strain tensor, we use the standard Le Dret-Raoult semidefinite projection formula for the quasiconvex envelope of the energy function to prove that there is no relaxation gap between the original non-convex calculus of variations problem and its linear moment formulation based on occupation measures. This implies convergence of the Lasserre moment-sum-of-squares (SOS) hierarchy and provides a computationally efficient, mesh-free numerical method that, unlike the finite element method, avoids undesirable mesh-dependent artifacts. Under the additional condition that the boundary condition is linear and the function is SOS convex in the strain tensor, we show that the first relaxation of the Lasserre hierarchy is exact. In other words, computing the quasiconvex envelope at a point boils down to solving a small convex semidefinite optimization problem.

</details>

Abstract: We study potential games on unimodular random graphs of bounded degree, where players interact through the underlying network. ### [143] [Gradient Descent's Last Iterate is Often (slightly) Suboptimal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13870)
*Guy Kornowski,Ohad Shamir*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在不知道时间范围T的情况下，梯度下降(GD)和随机梯度下降(SGD)的最后迭代无法达到最优的1/√T收敛率，必须承受额外的对数因子损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究凸Lipschitz函数优化中梯度下降和随机梯度下降的最后迭代收敛问题。Jain等人(2019)虽然构造了能达到最优1/√T收敛率的非标准步长序列，但需要预先知道总迭代次数T。作者旨在证明：在没有先验知识T的情况下，任何步长序列都无法确保SGD最后迭代达到最优误差。

Method: 通过理论证明方法，建立了在不知道时间范围T的情况下，梯度下降和随机梯度下降最后迭代收敛的下界。证明表明，即使在没有噪声的梯度下降情况下，任何时间(last iterate guarantee)的收敛保证也无法避免额外的多对数因子。

Result: 证明了Jain等人的猜想：在没有先验知识T的情况下，任何步长序列都无法确保SGD最后迭代达到最优的1/√T收敛率。即使在无噪声的GD情况下，任何时间的最后迭代保证也无法避免额外的poly-log(T)因子损失。证明还表明这种(略微)次优的停止时间在本质上是不可避免的。

Conclusion: 该研究为凸优化中最后迭代收敛的理论极限提供了重要洞见：在没有时间范围先验知识的情况下，梯度下降类算法的最后迭代收敛必然存在对数因子的理论下界，这揭示了优化算法设计中固有的权衡。

Abstract: We consider the well-studied setting of minimizing a convex Lipschitz function using either gradient descent (GD) or its stochastic variant (SGD), and examine the last iterate convergence. By now, it is known that standard stepsize choices lead to a last iterate convergence rate of $\log T/\sqrt{T}$ after $T$ steps. A breakthrough result of Jain et al. [2019] recovered the optimal $1/\sqrt{T}$ rate by constructing a non-standard stepsize sequence. However, this sequence requires choosing $T$ in advance, as opposed to common stepsize schedules which apply for any time horizon. Moreover, Jain et al. conjectured that without prior knowledge of $T$, no stepsize sequence can ensure the optimal error for SGD's last iterate, a claim which so far remained unproven. We prove this conjecture, and in fact show that even in the noiseless case of GD, it is impossible to avoid an excess poly-log factor in $T$ when considering an anytime last iterate guarantee. Our proof further suggests that such (slightly) suboptimal stopping times are unavoidably common.

### [146] [Understanding the Variance Dichotomy in Continuous Simulation Optimization: A Minimax Lower Bound Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.13965)
*Jianzhong Du,L. Jeff Hong*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 论文研究了连续模拟优化中的方差二分现象，揭示了在有限模拟预算下，低噪声随机CSO的复杂度与确定性CSO基本相同，但随着预算增加，收敛行为会过渡到由噪声方差和预算共同决定的较慢机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献显示确定性CSO与随机CSO之间存在显著对比，随机设置中的收敛率似乎对噪声方差大小不敏感。但这种渐近观点不能完全解释有限模拟预算下CSO的行为，特别是在低噪声设置中。需要填补这一研究空白。

Method: 开发了极小极大下界分析，证明复杂度由方差依赖项和方差独立项的最大值决定。通过理论分析揭示了在不同模拟预算和噪声方差条件下的复杂度变化规律。

Result: 当模拟预算不大且噪声方差较低时，方差独立项占主导，意味着低噪声随机CSO的复杂度与确定性CSO基本相同。随着预算增加，方差依赖项变得主导，随机CSO的收敛行为过渡到由噪声方差和模拟预算共同决定的较慢机制。

Conclusion: 连续模拟优化中存在方差二分现象，有限预算下的复杂度行为与渐近分析不同。低噪声随机CSO在有限预算下表现出与确定性CSO相似的复杂度特征，但随着预算增加会过渡到不同的收敛机制。

Abstract: This paper studies the variance dichotomy in continuous simulation optimization (CSO). Existing literature shows a sharp contrast between deterministic CSO and stochastic CSO, with convergence rates in stochastic settings appearing insensitive to the magnitude of the noise variance. However, this asymptotic view does not fully explain the behavior of CSO under finite simulation budgets, especially in low-noise settings. To address this gap, this work develops a minimax lower-bound analysis and shows that the complexity is decided by the maximum of a variance-dependent term and a variance-independent term. When the simulation budget is not very large and the noise variance is low, the variance-independent term dominates, implying that low-noise stochastic CSO has essentially the same complexity as deterministic CSO. As the budget increases, the variance-dependent term becomes dominant, and the convergence behavior of stochastic CSO transitions to a slower regime determined jointly by the noise variance and the simulation budget.

Motivation: 在插值型假设（如强增长条件）下，随机优化方法虽能达到与全批量方法相当的收敛速率，但性能（特别是SGD）对步长选择高度敏感。需要消除手动步长调优并扩展到约束问题。

Method: 提出统一随机信赖域框架：对于无约束优化，开发一阶随机信赖域算法；对于等式约束问题，引入基于二次罚函数的随机信赖域方法，使用罚参数μ。两种方法均自动调整步长，无需手动调优。

Result: 在强增长条件下，无约束算法达到O(ε^{-2}log(1/ε))的迭代和随机一阶oracle复杂度以找到ε-平稳点；约束方法达到O(ε^{-4}log(1/ε))复杂度以到达惩罚问题的ε-平稳点，对应原始约束问题的O(ε)-近似KKT点。

Conclusion: 提出的方法在深度神经网络训练和正交约束子空间拟合实验中，达到与精心调优的随机基线相当的性能，同时表现出稳定的优化行为，有效处理硬约束而无需手动学习率调度。

Abstract: Under interpolation-type assumptions such as the strong growth condition, stochastic optimization methods can attain convergence rates comparable to full-batch methods, but their performance, particularly for SGD, remains highly sensitive to step-size selection. To address this issue, we propose a unified stochastic trust-region framework that eliminates manual step-size tuning and extends naturally to equality-constrained problems. For unconstrained optimization, we develop a first-order stochastic trust-region algorithm and show that, under the strong growth condition, it achieves an iteration and stochastic first-order oracle complexity of $O(\varepsilon^{-2} \log(1/\varepsilon))$ for finding an $\varepsilon$-stationary point. For equality-constrained problems, we introduce a quadratic-penalty-based stochastic trust-region method with penalty parameter $μ$, and establish an iteration and oracle complexity of $O(\varepsilon^{-4} \log(1/\varepsilon))$ to reach an $\varepsilon$-stationary point of the penalized problem, corresponding to an $O(\varepsilon)$-approximate KKT point of the original constrained problem. Numerical experiments on deep neural network training and orthogonally constrained subspace fitting demonstrate that the proposed methods achieve performance comparable to well-tuned stochastic baselines, while exhibiting stable optimization behavior and effectively handling hard constraints without manual learning-rate scheduling.

</details>
